",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"require"}]," is used for general (normal) errors — such as errors that occur based on user input. ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"require"}]," does have the option for an error string. ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"revert"}]," is very similar to ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"require"}]," except that ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"revert"}]," will be called in ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"if ... else"}]," chains.
